\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00100}00100 \textcolor{comment}{/* The next sections is a series of control \#defines.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00101}00101 \textcolor{comment}{** various aspects of the generated parser.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00102}00102 \textcolor{comment}{**    YYCODETYPE         is the data type used to store the integer codes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00103}00103 \textcolor{comment}{**                       that represent terminal and non-\/terminal symbols.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00104}00104 \textcolor{comment}{**                       "{}unsigned char"{} is used if there are fewer than}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00105}00105 \textcolor{comment}{**                       256 symbols.  Larger types otherwise.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00106}00106 \textcolor{comment}{**    YYNOCODE           is a number of type YYCODETYPE that is not used for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00107}00107 \textcolor{comment}{**                       any terminal or nonterminal symbol.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00108}00108 \textcolor{comment}{**    YYFALLBACK         If defined, this indicates that one or more tokens}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00109}00109 \textcolor{comment}{**                       (also known as: "{}terminal symbols"{}) have fall-\/back}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00110}00110 \textcolor{comment}{**                       values which should be used if the original symbol}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00111}00111 \textcolor{comment}{**                       would not parse.  This permits keywords to sometimes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00112}00112 \textcolor{comment}{**                       be used as identifiers, for example.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00113}00113 \textcolor{comment}{**    YYACTIONTYPE       is the data type used for "{}action codes"{} -\/ numbers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00114}00114 \textcolor{comment}{**                       that indicate what to do in response to the next}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00115}00115 \textcolor{comment}{**                       token.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00116}00116 \textcolor{comment}{**    ParseTOKENTYPE     is the data type used for minor type for terminal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00117}00117 \textcolor{comment}{**                       symbols.  Background: A "{}minor type"{} is a semantic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00118}00118 \textcolor{comment}{**                       value associated with a terminal or non-\/terminal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00119}00119 \textcolor{comment}{**                       symbols.  For example, for an "{}ID"{} terminal symbol,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00120}00120 \textcolor{comment}{**                       the minor type might be the name of the identifier.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00121}00121 \textcolor{comment}{**                       Each non-\/terminal can have a different minor type.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00122}00122 \textcolor{comment}{**                       Terminal symbols all have the same minor type, though.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00123}00123 \textcolor{comment}{**                       This macros defines the minor type for terminal }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00124}00124 \textcolor{comment}{**                       symbols.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00125}00125 \textcolor{comment}{**    YYMINORTYPE        is the data type used for all minor types.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00126}00126 \textcolor{comment}{**                       This is typically a union of many types, one of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00127}00127 \textcolor{comment}{**                       which is ParseTOKENTYPE.  The entry in the union}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00128}00128 \textcolor{comment}{**                       for terminal symbols is called "{}yy0"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00129}00129 \textcolor{comment}{**    YYSTACKDEPTH       is the maximum depth of the parser's stack.  If}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00130}00130 \textcolor{comment}{**                       zero the stack is dynamically sized using realloc()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00131}00131 \textcolor{comment}{**    ParseARG\_SDECL     A static variable declaration for the \%extra\_argument}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00132}00132 \textcolor{comment}{**    ParseARG\_PDECL     A parameter declaration for the \%extra\_argument}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00133}00133 \textcolor{comment}{**    ParseARG\_PARAM     Code to pass \%extra\_argument as a subroutine parameter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00134}00134 \textcolor{comment}{**    ParseARG\_STORE     Code to store \%extra\_argument into yypParser}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00135}00135 \textcolor{comment}{**    ParseARG\_FETCH     Code to extract \%extra\_argument from yypParser}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00136}00136 \textcolor{comment}{**    ParseCTX\_*         As ParseARG\_ except for \%extra\_context}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00137}00137 \textcolor{comment}{**    YYERRORSYMBOL      is the code number of the error symbol.  If not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00138}00138 \textcolor{comment}{**                       defined, then do no error processing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00139}00139 \textcolor{comment}{**    YYNSTATE           the combined number of states.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00140}00140 \textcolor{comment}{**    YYNRULE            the number of rules in the grammar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00141}00141 \textcolor{comment}{**    YYNTOKEN           Number of terminal symbols}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00142}00142 \textcolor{comment}{**    YY\_MAX\_SHIFT       Maximum value for shift actions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00143}00143 \textcolor{comment}{**    YY\_MIN\_SHIFTREDUCE Minimum value for shift-\/reduce actions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00144}00144 \textcolor{comment}{**    YY\_MAX\_SHIFTREDUCE Maximum value for shift-\/reduce actions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00145}00145 \textcolor{comment}{**    YY\_ERROR\_ACTION    The yy\_action[] code for syntax error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00146}00146 \textcolor{comment}{**    YY\_ACCEPT\_ACTION   The yy\_action[] code for accept}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00147}00147 \textcolor{comment}{**    YY\_NO\_ACTION       The yy\_action[] code for no-\/op}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00148}00148 \textcolor{comment}{**    YY\_MIN\_REDUCE      Minimum value for reduce actions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00149}00149 \textcolor{comment}{**    YY\_MAX\_REDUCE      Maximum value for reduce actions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00150}00150 \textcolor{comment}{*/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00191}00191 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00192}00192 \textcolor{comment}{/* Define the yytestcase() macro to be a no-\/op if is not already defined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00193}00193 \textcolor{comment}{** otherwise.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00194}00194 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00195}00195 \textcolor{comment}{** Applications can choose to define yytestcase() in the \%include section}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00196}00196 \textcolor{comment}{** to a macro that can assist in verifying code coverage.  For production}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00197}00197 \textcolor{comment}{** code the yytestcase() macro should be turned off.  But it is useful}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00198}00198 \textcolor{comment}{** for testing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00199}00199 \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00200}00200 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef yytestcase}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00201}\mbox{\hyperlink{parser_8c_09_09_a9dcaf5b61f785198ed3ea047a7c621a7}{00201}} \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# define yytestcase(X)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00202}00202 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00203}00203 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00204}00204 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00205}00205 \textcolor{comment}{/* Next are the tables used to determine what action to take based on the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00206}00206 \textcolor{comment}{** current state and lookahead token.  These tables are used to implement}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00207}00207 \textcolor{comment}{** functions that take a state number and lookahead value and return an}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00208}00208 \textcolor{comment}{** action integer.  }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00209}00209 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00210}00210 \textcolor{comment}{** Suppose the action integer is N.  Then the action is determined as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00211}00211 \textcolor{comment}{** follows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00212}00212 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00213}00213 \textcolor{comment}{**   0 <= N <= YY\_MAX\_SHIFT             Shift N.  That is, push the lookahead}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00214}00214 \textcolor{comment}{**                                      token onto the stack and goto state N.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00215}00215 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00216}00216 \textcolor{comment}{**   N between YY\_MIN\_SHIFTREDUCE       Shift to an arbitrary state then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00217}00217 \textcolor{comment}{**     and YY\_MAX\_SHIFTREDUCE           reduce by rule N-\/YY\_MIN\_SHIFTREDUCE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00218}00218 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00219}00219 \textcolor{comment}{**   N == YY\_ERROR\_ACTION               A syntax error has occurred.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00220}00220 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00221}00221 \textcolor{comment}{**   N == YY\_ACCEPT\_ACTION              The parser accepts its input.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00222}00222 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00223}00223 \textcolor{comment}{**   N == YY\_NO\_ACTION                  No such action.  Denotes unused}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00224}00224 \textcolor{comment}{**                                      slots in the yy\_action[] table.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00225}00225 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00226}00226 \textcolor{comment}{**   N between YY\_MIN\_REDUCE            Reduce by rule N-\/YY\_MIN\_REDUCE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00227}00227 \textcolor{comment}{**     and YY\_MAX\_REDUCE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00228}00228 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00229}00229 \textcolor{comment}{** The action table is constructed as a single large table named yy\_action[].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00230}00230 \textcolor{comment}{** Given state S and lookahead X, the action is computed as either:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00231}00231 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00232}00232 \textcolor{comment}{**    (A)   N = yy\_action[ yy\_shift\_ofst[S] + X ]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00233}00233 \textcolor{comment}{**    (B)   N = yy\_default[S]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00234}00234 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00235}00235 \textcolor{comment}{** The (A) formula is preferred.  The B formula is used instead if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00236}00236 \textcolor{comment}{** yy\_lookahead[yy\_shift\_ofst[S]+X] is not equal to X.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00237}00237 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00238}00238 \textcolor{comment}{** The formulas above are for computing the action when the lookahead is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00239}00239 \textcolor{comment}{** a terminal symbol.  If the lookahead is a non-\/terminal (as occurs after}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00240}00240 \textcolor{comment}{** a reduce action) then the yy\_reduce\_ofst[] array is used in place of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00241}00241 \textcolor{comment}{** the yy\_shift\_ofst[] array.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00242}00242 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00243}00243 \textcolor{comment}{** The following are the tables generated in this section:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00244}00244 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00245}00245 \textcolor{comment}{**  yy\_action[]        A single table containing all actions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00246}00246 \textcolor{comment}{**  yy\_lookahead[]     A table containing the lookahead for each entry in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00247}00247 \textcolor{comment}{**                     yy\_action.  Used to detect hash collisions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00248}00248 \textcolor{comment}{**  yy\_shift\_ofst[]    For each state, the offset into yy\_action for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00249}00249 \textcolor{comment}{**                     shifting terminals.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00250}00250 \textcolor{comment}{**  yy\_reduce\_ofst[]   For each state, the offset into yy\_action for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00251}00251 \textcolor{comment}{**                     shifting non-\/terminals after a reduce.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00252}00252 \textcolor{comment}{**  yy\_default[]       Default action for each state.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00253}00253 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00254}00254 \textcolor{comment}{*********** Begin parsing tables **********************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00255}\mbox{\hyperlink{parser_8c_09_09_a66999188dbe38a1633033ed380c61159}{00255}} \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define YY\_ACTTAB\_COUNT (1979)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00751}00751 \textcolor{comment}{/* The next table maps tokens (terminal symbols) into fallback tokens.  }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00752}00752 \textcolor{comment}{** If a construct like the following:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00753}00753 \textcolor{comment}{** }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00754}00754 \textcolor{comment}{**      \%fallback ID X Y Z.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00755}00755 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00756}00756 \textcolor{comment}{** appears in the grammar, then ID becomes a fallback token for X, Y,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00757}00757 \textcolor{comment}{** and Z.  Whenever one of the tokens X, Y, or Z is input to the parser}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00758}00758 \textcolor{comment}{** but it does not parse, the type of the token is changed to ID and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00759}00759 \textcolor{comment}{** the parse is retried before an error is thrown.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00760}00760 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00761}00761 \textcolor{comment}{** This feature can be used, for example, to cause some keywords in a language}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00762}00762 \textcolor{comment}{** to revert to identifiers if they keyword does not apply in the context where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00763}00763 \textcolor{comment}{** it appears.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00764}00764 \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00765}00765 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef YYFALLBACK}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00868}00868 \textcolor{comment}{/* }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00869}00869 \textcolor{comment}{** Turn parser tracing on by giving a stream to which to write the trace}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00870}00870 \textcolor{comment}{** and a prompt to preface each trace message.  Tracing is turned off}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00871}00871 \textcolor{comment}{** by making either argument NULL }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00872}00872 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00873}00873 \textcolor{comment}{** Inputs:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00874}00874 \textcolor{comment}{** <ul>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00875}00875 \textcolor{comment}{** <li> A FILE* to which trace output should be written.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00876}00876 \textcolor{comment}{**      If NULL, then tracing is turned off.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00877}00877 \textcolor{comment}{** <li> A prefix string written at the beginning of every}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00878}00878 \textcolor{comment}{**      line of trace output.  If NULL, then tracing is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00879}00879 \textcolor{comment}{**      turned off.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00880}00880 \textcolor{comment}{** </ul>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00881}00881 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l00882}00882 \textcolor{comment}{** Outputs:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l02613}02613 \textcolor{comment}{      **}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l02614}02614 \textcolor{comment}{      ** This is what we do if the grammar does define ERROR:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l02615}02615 \textcolor{comment}{      **}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l02616}02616 \textcolor{comment}{      **  * Call the \%syntax\_error function.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l02619}02619 \textcolor{comment}{      **    it is legal to shift the error symbol, then shift}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l02620}02620 \textcolor{comment}{      **    the error symbol.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l02621}02621 \textcolor{comment}{      **}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l02623}02623 \textcolor{comment}{      **}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l02624}02624 \textcolor{comment}{      **  * Begin accepting and shifting new tokens.  No new error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l02625}02625 \textcolor{comment}{      **    processing will occur until three tokens have been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l02626}02626 \textcolor{comment}{      **    shifted successfully.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l02627}02627 \textcolor{comment}{      **}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{parser_8c_09_09_source_l02628}02628 \textcolor{comment}{      */}}
